\DoxyCodeLine{02052\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ separate\ type\ would\ result\ in\ shorter\ symbols\ but\ break\ ABI\ compatibility}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02053\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ clang\ and\ gcc\ on\ ARM\ (\#1919).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02054\ FMT\_EXPORT\ \textcolor{keyword}{using\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__format__args}{format\_args}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__format__args}{basic\_format\_args<format\_context>}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{02056\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ cannot\ use\ enum\ classes\ as\ bit\ fields\ because\ of\ a\ gcc\ bug,\ so\ we\ put\ them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02057\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ namespaces\ instead\ (https://gcc.gnu.org/bugzilla/show\_bug.cgi?id=61414).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02058\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Additionally,\ if\ an\ underlying\ type\ is\ specified,\ older\ gcc\ incorrectly\ warns}}
